The next day, we went to Huabang Hotel for breakfast. The buffet variety was slightly less and the taste was average. This may be the only regret of this stay.
When checking out, the housekeeper Xiao Jiang also gave fruit and mineral water. Overall, this stay was very pleasant and enjoyable. I will come again next time, especially the work of the housekeeper Xiao Jiang deserves praise

name:A‚Äçi‚Äçm‚Äça‚Äço‚Äçx‚Äçi‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äçd‚Äçe‚Äçy‚Äça‚Äçy‚Äça

info:15 Reviews
rating:3.7
posted:Posted February 19, 2024
msg:Don't go to Disney in summer, don't go to Zhuoya in winter. Expand: I stayed in Huabang for two days and Zhuoya for one day. Both hotels belong to the same group and are located in the front and back of the scenic area. From the location: Zhuoya is in the front, and some rooms are 50 meters behind the small train section. Huabang is in the back and closer to the VIP channel. From the front desk service: Huabang has more KPI pressure, and the service is more diligent and experienced. I want to thank Manager Yang of Zhuoya! Actively help to solve problems! From the facilities: Huabang's room is small, so the floor heating is very powerful! Zhuoya's smallest room is large, and the floor heating cannot meet normal needs. The hot water is not hot, and I shiver when taking a shower in winter. The worst thing is that the room I stayed in has a smell of sewage. I woke up in the middle of the night! And the smell came from under the floor on the side of the bed near the bathroom. From the perspective of quietness and privacy, there are too many people in Huabang, and the control of outsiders is not strict. Locals also run in to play in the snow through the VIP channel. The door access control of Zhuoya has been closed, and there are fewer unrelated outsiders, which is quieter. So, comprehensively speaking, I believe that Zhuoya should have a great advantage in warm climates, especially in summer.
